msg:advantage:
1. The room is big. This is determined by the room type. Looking at the evacuation plan, there are only four rooms on the first floor of ordinary floors. The advantage of a larger room is that it has a separate large table, which is more suitable for families with older children.
2. Good service. It goes without saying that it is a five-star hotel, and the attitude is very good. Of course the front desk doorman could be more proactive. The front desk manager saw us taking care of our children and immediately gave them a set of balloon accessories to express our gratitude.
3. The door card is unique. The wooden door card looks very exquisite. I even kept one as a souvenir.
4. The swimming pool is good, with three 25-meter swimming lanes and an irregular paddling pool next to it. The depth of 1.4 meters is sufficient, the water is quite clean, and the water temperature is also suitable. It is recommended not to fix the depth. The paddling pool can be shallower to facilitate children's play in the water.
5. The location is good, it takes 15 minutes to walk to the beach and 30 minutes to the north gate of Yantai University.
Here are the disadvantages:
1. The hotel is really a bit old. When you enter the room, there is a smell of age, which is not very good. Two of the three sliding doors in the room could not be pushed.
2. Room service calls often require waiting. Although the service is very good, it always takes a minute or so for someone to answer the phone.
3. Shampoo, etc. are actually in such large bottles. This is the first time I've seen this used in a five-star hotel. It's a configuration only found in fast hotels, and it's very unhygienic. By the way, the thermostatic faucet is good, but it is too old, does not look clean, and the temperature adjus**ent is not stuck in place. It is easy to misoperate and cause the water temperature to be too high. The water temperature in the sink was not warm enough, there was only warm water but no hot water.
4. The minibar is empty and not good for the senses.
